--
-- Table structure for table `benchmark_testcases`
--

  `id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `request_type` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `context_type` varchar(2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `url` mediumtext NOT NULL,
  `category` mediumtext,
  `description` mediumtext,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=5053 ;

--
-- Table structure for table `benchmark_testcase_times`
--

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `benchmark_testcase_times` (
  `id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `benchmark_container_id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `testcases_id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `time_process` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `time_parse` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `time_fetch` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`,`benchmark_container_id`,`testcases_id`),
  KEY `fk_tescase_times_benchmark_container` (`benchmark_container_id`),
  KEY `fk_tescase_times_testcases1` (`testcases_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=17701 ;
